LEGEND:
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Res #     : Sequential residue number
ID        : Residue amino acid code (ALA, GLN, etc.)
Num       : Residue number from PDB file
DSSP ASA  : DSSP accessible surface area (Ų)
DSSP Class: DSSP classification (1=exterior ≥30Ų, 0=interior <30Ų)
DSSP SS   : DSSP secondary structure (H=helix, E=strand, C=coil, etc.)
STRIDE ASA: STRIDE accessible surface area (Ų)
STRIDE Class: STRIDE classification (1=exterior ≥24Ų, 0=interior <24Ų)
STRIDE SS : STRIDE secondary structure
NC6       : Neighbor count within 6Å sphere
Uni6      : Uniformity at 6Å (spherical variance, 0-1)
NC10      : Neighbor count within 10Å sphere
Uni10     : Uniformity at 10Å (spherical variance, 0-1)
NCPS Class: Our classification (1=exterior, 0=interior)

CLASSIFICATION PARAMETERS:
  - nc6_threshold = 6 (minimum neighbors at 6Å)
  - nc10_threshold = 12 (minimum neighbors at 10Å)
  - uni6_threshold = 0.30 (minimum uniformity at 6Å)
  - uni10_threshold = 0.60 (minimum uniformity at 10Å)
  - Exterior if: NC6 < 6 OR NC10 < 12 OR Uni6 < 0.30 OR Uni10 < 0.60
  - Interior otherwise
